However, it's important to note that the statement "sea level rise does not seem to depend on ocean temperature and certainly not on CO2" is not supported by the scientific consensus. Sea level rise is primarily driven by the melting of glaciers and ice caps, which is influenced by both ocean temperature and atmospheric CO2 levels. The misconception may arise from a lack of understanding of the complex interactions between these factors.
